\[
F(t,A)=0.2331857324\,A^{1/3}\;-\;0.3115334933\,A^2\;-\;0.3115334933\,A\,e^{-0.08476196603\,t}.

So any matching candidate must be able to represent **exactly three terms**: an \(A^{1/3}\) term, an \(A^2\) term, and an \(A e^{kt}\) term with \(k=-0.08476196603\), and **no extra dependence** on \(t\) or \(A\) (no constants, logs, denominators, abs, etc.) after parameter choices.

---

### 1. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5/(A**c4 + c6) + c7`
Has a rational term \(A^{c4}c5/(A^{c4}+c6)\) which cannot become a pure power \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\) unless \(c5=0\) (then it vanishes). Then remaining terms are \(A e^{c1 t}\) and \(A^{c2}\), but GT needs both \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\). Only one power term available ⇒ cannot match.

### 2. `A**(1/3)*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4/(c5*t + c6) + c7 + c8/(c5*t + c6)`
Extra terms with \((c5 t+c6)^{-1}\) depend on \(t\) in a non-exponential way. Only way to remove them for all \(t\) is set \(c4=0\) and \(c8=0\). Also must set \(c7=0\). Then it becomes exactly \(c0 A^{1/3}+c1 A^2 + c2 A e^{c3 t}\), which can match GT by choosing constants appropriately. **Matches.**

One valid assignment:
- \(c0=0.2331857324078805\)
- \(c1=-0.3115334933234426\)
- \(c2=-0.3115334933234426\)
- \(c3=-0.08476196603472734\)
- \(c4=0,\;c7=0,\;c8=0\) (and \(c5,c6\) arbitrary)

### 3. `A**(1/3)*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*Abs(A)**c7`
Has an extra constant \(c4\) (set \(c4=0\)). Also extra term \(c5 e^{c6 t}|A|^{c7}\) must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Then reduces to the needed 3-term form ⇒ can match (same parameter choices as #2 for the first three terms). **Matches.**

### 4. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`
Has two power terms \(A^{c2}\) and \(A^{c4}\) plus an \(A e^{c1 t}\), good in principle, but also has \(c6\) and a pure \(e^{c8 t}\) term independent of \(A\). ### 6. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5 + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t)`

### 15. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A**c2*c3 + A**c4*c5 + c6`

### 19. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A*c3 + A**c4*c5 + c6`
Set \(c3=0\), \(c6=0\), choose \(c4=1/3,c5=0.233185...\), and match other coefficients/exponent. **Matches.**

### 20. `... + A*c4 + c5`
Extra linear \(A\) term and constant; set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 21. `... + A**2*c2 + A*c3 + A*c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Has extra \(A^2\) term and linear \(A\) term and constant. Set \(c2=0,c3=0,c6=0\). Then 3-term form with \(A*c4 e^{c5 t}\) as the exponential term ⇒ **Matches.**

### 22. `... + c4 + c5*Abs(A)**(2/3)`
Set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 23. `... + c4 + c5*sqrt(Abs(A))`
Set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 24. `... + A*c4*(c5 + t)**c6 + c7`
The extra term has \((t+c5)^{c6}\) non-exponential; must set \(c4=0\). Also set \(c7=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 25. `... + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t)*Abs(A)`
Set \(c4=0\). The extra term is another \(A e^{c6 t}\)-type but with Abs(A); to avoid mismatch for all real \(A\), set \(c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 26. `... + A**c4*c5*exp(c6/(c7 + t)) + c8`
The \(e^{c6/(c7+t)}\) dependence cannot be removed except by setting \(c5=0\). Also set \(c8=0\). Then only \(A e^{...}\) and one power remain ⇒ cannot match.

### 27. `... + c4 + c5*log(c6*exp(A**c7*c8 + c9*t) + 1)`
Log-of-exp term cannot become a pure power/exponential sum; must set \(c5=0\). Then you have \(A e^{...}\) and one power plus constant \(c4\) (set \(c4=0\)). Still missing one of the two power terms ⇒ cannot match.

### 28. `... + A**c4*c5/(A**c6*c7 + 1) + c8`
Rational-in-\(A\) term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Also set \(c8=0\). Then only \(A e^{...}\) and one power remain ⇒ cannot match.

### 29. `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c0*c4 + A**c5*c6*exp(A*c7)*exp(c8*t) + c9`
Extra term with \(e^{A c7}\) must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c9=0\). Remaining gives two power terms tied to same exponent \(c0\): \(c1 A^{c0+1}\) and \(c4 A^{c0}\). To get \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\) would require \(c0+1=2\Rightarrow c0=1\) and \(c0=1/3\) simultaneously ⇒ impossible. No match.

### 30. `... + c4 + c5*exp(c6*t) + c7*exp(c8*t)*Abs(A)**c9`
Pure \(e^{c6 t}\) term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Extra \(e^{c8 t}|A|^{c9}\) must vanish: set \(c7=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then only \(A e^{...}\) and one power remain ⇒ cannot match.

### 31. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*log(c5*exp(A**c6*c7) + 1)`
Log term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c3=0\). Then only \(A^2\) and \(A e^{...}\), missing \(A^{1/3}\) ⇒ no match.

### 32. `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c0*c4 + A**c5*c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8`
Log term must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Same exponent-coupling issue as #29: powers are \(A^{c0+1}\) and \(A^{c0}\) only, cannot yield both \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\). No match.

### 33. `... + A**c5*c6*cos(c7*t) + c8`
Cos term must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Remaining has coupled exponents \(A^{c0+1}\) and \(A^{c0}\) again ⇒ cannot match. No match.

### 34. `A**(1/3)*c0 + A**2*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t)`
Already exactly the same functional form as GT. Choose
\(c0=0.2331857324,\;c1=-0.3115334933,\;c2=-0.3115334933,\;c3=-0.08476196603\).
**Matches.**

### 35. `... + c4 + c5*log(c6*exp(c7*Abs(A)) + 1)`
Log term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 36. `... + c4*exp(c5*t) + c6`
Extra pure exponential and constant; set \(c4=0,c6=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 37. `... + c4*t**c5 + c6`
Extra \(t^{c5}\) term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c6=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 38. `... + c4*log(c5*t + 1) + c6`
Log-in-\(t\) term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c6=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 39. `... + c4 + c5*t`
Extra constant and linear-in-\(t\) term; set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 40. `... + c4*sin(A*c5 + c6) + c7`
Sin term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c7=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 41. `... + c4 + c5*Abs(A)*Max(0, c6 + t)`
Piecewise Max term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 42. `... + A**2*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5`
Extra \(A^2\) term can be absorbed by setting \(c2=0\) (or adjusting with \(c1\)), but constant \(c5\) must be 0. Then it’s 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 43. `... + c4 + c5*Abs(A)**2`
Set \(c4=0,c5=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 44. `... + c4`
Set \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 45. `A**(1/3)*c0 + A**2*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t)*Abs(A)`
Abs(A) exponential term cannot equal \(A e^{kt}\) for all real \(A\) unless you restrict domain; equivalence here is for all \(A\). Best is set \(c3=0\), then you lose the needed \(A e^{kt}\) term. So cannot match.

### 46. `A**2*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + c3 + c4*Abs(A)**(1/3)`
Abs(A)^(1/3) cannot equal \(A^{1/3}\) for negative \(A\). If we set \(c4=0\), we lose the \(A^{1/3}\) term. If we keep it, mismatch on sign. Thus no match for all real \(A\).

### 47. `... + c4 + c5*t*(A + c6)**c7`
Extra mixed \(t\) and \(A\) power term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 48. `... + c4*t/(A*c5 + c6) + c7/(A*c5 + c6) + c8`
Extra rational-in-\(A\) terms must vanish: set \(c4=0,c7=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 49. `... + c4*exp(A*c5) + c6`
Extra \(e^{A c5}\) term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c6=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 50. `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c0*c4 + A**c5*c6 + c7`
Constant \(c7=0\). Still has coupled exponents \(A^{c0+1}\) and \(A^{c0}\) plus another power \(A^{c5}\). Could we get \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\)? If set \(c0=1/3\), then \(A^{c0}=A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{c0+1}=A^{4/3}\) (unwanted unless coefficient 0). You could set \(c1=0\) to kill \(A^{4/3}\), keep \(A^{1/3}\) via \(c4\), and set \(c5=2\) for \(A^2\). Then plus the \(A e^{c3 t}\) term. This works. **Matches.**

### 51. `A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A**c3 + c4) + A**c5*c6 + c7`
Rational term \(A*c2/(A^{c3}+c4)\) cannot become a pure \(A^2\) or \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\); must set \(c2=0\). Then only one power term \(A^{c5}\) remains besides the exponential term; cannot get both \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\). No match.

### 52. `... + c4 + c5*log(c6*exp(A**c7*c8) + 1)`
Log term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 53. `A*c0 + A*c1*exp(c2*t) + A**c3*c4 + A**c5*c6 + c7`
Has an extra linear \(A\) term \(A*c0\) (set \(c0=0\)) and constant \(c7=0\). Then two power terms and one \(A e^{...}\) term remain; choose exponents \(c3=2\), \(c5=1/3\) with appropriate coefficients. **Matches.**

### 54. `... + A**c4*c5 + c6*Abs(A) + c7`
Abs(A) term must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c7=0\). Then same as #15: can choose \(c2=2\), \(c4=1/3\). **Matches.**

### 55. `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A*c4*(A + c5)**c6 + A**c0*c7 + c8`
The \(A*c4*(A+c5)^{c6}\) term cannot be made a pure power for all \(A\) unless removed: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Remaining has coupled exponents \(A^{c0+1}\) and \(A^{c0}\) only; cannot yield both \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\) simultaneously. No match.

### 56. `A**2*c0 + A*A**c1*c2 + A*c3*exp(c4*t) + A*c5 + A**c1*c6 + c7`
Has powers \(A^{c1+1}\) and \(A^{c1}\) plus unwanted linear \(A*c5\) and constant \(c7\). Set \(c5=0,c7=0\). To get \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^2\): set \(c1=1/3\) gives \(A^{c1}=A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{c1+1}=A^{4/3}\) (must kill by setting \(c2=0\)), while \(A^2\) comes from the explicit \(A^2*c0\). Then match coefficients and exponential term. Works. **Matches.**

### 57. `A*A**c0*c1 + A*c2*exp(c3*t) + A**c0*c4 + A**c5*c6*exp(c7*t) + c8`
Extra term \(A^{c5} e^{c7 t}\) must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Remaining has coupled exponents \(A^{c0+1}\) and \(A^{c0}\) only ⇒ cannot produce both \(A^2\) and \(A^{1/3}\). No match.

### 58. `... + A*c4/(A*c5 + c6) + c7/(A*c5 + c6) + c8`
Extra rational-in-\(A\) terms must vanish: set \(c4=0,c7=0\). Constant \(c8=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 59. `... + c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6`
Log(A) term must vanish: set \(c4=0\). Constant \(c6=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 60. `... + c4 + c5*cos(c6*t)*Abs(A)**c7`
Cos term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 61. `... + A**c2*c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5 + c6*exp(A*c7)*Abs(A)**c8`
Log term must vanish: set \(c3=0\). Extra \(e^{A c7}\) term must vanish: set \(c6=0\). Constant \(c5=0\). Then only \(A e^{...}\) remains ⇒ cannot match.

### 62. `... + c4 + c5*cos(c6*log(c7*exp(c8*t) + 1))`
Extra oscillatory-in-\(t\) term must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 63. `... + c4 + c5*exp(c6*cos(c7*t))`
Extra nontrivial \(t\)-dependence must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**

### 64. `... + c4 + c5*sin(c6*t + c7)`
Extra sinusoid must vanish: set \(c5=0\). Constant \(c4=0\). Then 3-term form ⇒ **Matches.**
